commit 950d200342e5d84ff9d85bc872c201d1c099f507
Author: Ryan Rossiter <rlrossit@us.ibm.com>
Date:   2018-01-24 13:45:52 -0600

    Add fix for unsetting of values in edit SG rules
    
    The SL API for editing security group rules allows you to unset string
    values by passing in an empty string (''). The edit_securitygroup_rule()
    function skipped over any values that were falsy (because if they
    weren't set in the arguments, we don't want to change them).
    Unfortunately, this caused values that were an empty string to also get
    skipped over and not get unset in the API. So edit needs to check
    explicitly for None (don't change) in order to get skipped over in
    passing to the API.

7	7	SoftLayer/managers/network.py
17	0	tests/managers/network_tests.py

commit 74830b54aa19eb1f83d311fb0e63b07c9953e090
Author: David Pickle <dpickle29@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-12-05 16:56:57 -0600

    Fix parsing logic in volume-detail commands to handle invalid types
    
    Some certain types of transactions which are currently returned in
    a volume's activeTransactions contain transactionStatus sub-properties
    of inconsistent types. There is a plan to fix the core issue in the
    backend, but until that fix is added, the changes in this commit
    should prevent the volume-detail commands from resulting in an
    error if any invalid transactionStatus objects are returned.

Date:   2017-11-30 16:07:41 -0600

    Update needed fixes for CLI and add doc
    
    The CLI appears to fail out if it gets AttributeError as part of any of
    the manager calls, so in order to not make it look like a
    softlayer-pythyon but, we need to spit out something from
    SoftLayer.exceptions. The base exceptions.SoftLayerError was used.

    both the activePresets and accountRestrictedActivePresets need to be
    retrieved and merged together before being returned.
    
    Finally, extra doc was added to verify_order() and place_order() to
    make it easier to understand how to use it.

commit ab5ba938792df9a9aa5f69edc720adbe670ee64a
Author: Ryan Rossiter <rlrossit@us.ibm.com>
Date:   2017-11-22 14:37:48 -0600

    Add ordering APIs and commands
    
    This change adds a new command, and 5 new subcommands:
    
    slcli order - command for interacting with the ordering API
    
    slcli order category-list -- subcommand for listing categories in a
    package
    
    slcli order item-list -- subcommand for listing items in a package
    
    slcli order package-list -- subcommand for listing available packages
    
    slcli order place -- subcommand for verifying/placing orders
    
    slcli order preset-list -- subcommand for listing presets of a package
    
    API functions in SoftLayer.managers.ordering.OrderingManager were also
    added to programmatically interact with all of these functions as well.
    
    The place_order() and verify_order() commands are built to pass a
    package keyname, a location, and a list of item keynames. It then
    transforms the keynames into IDs, which the place/verifyOrder APIs
    accept.

commit 35f5799daedba22ba2b4747da77ab93c1edb357b
Author: Ryan Rossiter <rlrossit@us.ibm.com>
Date:   2017-05-02 15:59:22 -0500

    Set formatting.blank() properly
    
    Because some of the .get() calls return an empty string, they're not
    actually getting filled with formatting.blank(). This changes the get()
    calls to add the or after the get() call. This way, if the returned
    value is empty string (so not set), we'll fill it with a
    formatting.blank() instead of filling it with nothing.

commit f72eee5be4eae04b93ce7f03c39d8eaa3d0fa996
Author: Ryan Rossiter <rlrossit@us.ibm.com>
Date:   2017-01-24 13:40:45 -0600

    Add security group functionality
    
    This adds security group API helpers to the network manager. This allows
    users to perform CRUD operations on security groups, security group
    rules, and interface attachments to security groups. CLI commands were
    also added to perform these API operations on the command line.
    
    Arguments were also added to the instance creation to allow VSIs to be
    booted with security groups on the public and/or private interfaces of
    the newly created VSI.
    
    Security group information was added to the VSI detail CLI, so the
    security groups attached to the interfaces of a VSI are output as part
    of the detail.

    Update file/block ordering to support storage_as_a_service package
    
    **Includes updates to logic for ordering volumes, replicas,
    and snapshot space. The storage_as_a_service package is used
    as a default for new volume orders, but customers can specify
    older packages for use. The package associated with the
    existing primary volume is used in replica and snapshot orders.

    for File and Block manager functions.

    Adds prompts for virtual and hardware server creation.
    
     * Environmental variables prefixed with "SLAPI_" can be used to default CLI options.
       For example, this will default to always using raw formatting:
    
    ```bash
    export SLCLI_FORMAT=raw
    slcli vs list
    ```
    
     * Fixes the --like option for creating virtual servers.
     * Changes how --like and --template options work to use more of click's feature-set.

commit 9acd37b8231642fc349c4b5babc2e554d6781f01
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-08-03 18:00:20 -0500

    Adds Shell / Moves fixtures
    
    This commit adds a shell that can be started by simply calling 'slcli' with no
    command. The shell can be exited using ctrl + d. The shell has autocomplete.
    The shell probably needs a way to set global options (--fixtures, --debug, --proxy,
    --config, --timings, etc). In the future, this mode can be used to prompt for user
    input.
    
    Fixtures were moved to a higher level to avoid needing test dependencies to use fixtures.

commit 42b9bd72149d4370faaa5de7c38abfd028365fee
Author: Kevin McDonald <kmcdonald@softlayer.com>
Date:   2015-07-28 15:26:37 -0500

    Better comforms to click.MultiCommand.get_command
    
    Usually click.MultiCommand.get_command will return None when the command is not found. In slcli,
    this is handled by raising an exception. Since click handles this condition for us, there's no
    reason it should be done here.
    
    Removes SoftLayer.CLI.InvalidCommand and its single reference

commit 3565bb79c1742deb65c799431749da3c381a1841
Author: Kevin McDonald <kmcdonald@softlayer.com>
Date:   2015-07-14 15:40:21 -0500

    Remove Python 2.6 Testing. Add python 3.5.
    
    Mock, the mocking library that is used to test with has stopped support
    python 2.6. This is now causing travis-ci builds to fail. This change removes
    python 2.6 from tox and adds python 3.5 since travis-ci now supports testing
    the beta version of python 3.5.

commit 9ad61e3f3c40b7212bf39666d97097aa7a50caaf
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-04-27 12:12:01 -0500

    Fixes a failing CLI setup test.
    
    This test is failing because of two PRs interacting in unexpected ways.
    One change changes the tests to use a real XML-RPC transport against a real HTTP
    server which responds with stubbed data. The other change fixes a bug where the endpoint
    being used to validate credentials was simply using the default.
    
    Now, the tests be sure to use a stubbed transport so that changing the endpoint will not
    cause `slcli setup` to use the default endpoint and make real API calls against it.

commit 498ad88d17c04061666dce0e1b9a34d5b40947f3
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2014-11-07 15:05:47 -0600

    Streamline virtual and hardware server listings.
    
    The listing accrued too much stuff and was causing normal listing
    to be way too wide. Additionally, masking in billing information
    in order to get the creator of the server added a significant amount
    of time to the API call.
    
    FQDN column -> just display hostname (without domain name).
    cores column -> removed
    memory column -> removed
    owner column -> removed
    
    Now, only the following columns are shown:
     * id
     * datacenter
     * hostname
     * primary_ip

commit 63b52c3002605a05f9a03fd396e9577e08132fd1
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2014-11-02 19:25:18 -0600

    Pluggable Transports
    
    This makes transports plugable. Things converted to transports:
     * SoftLayer.API.TimedClient -> SoftLayer.transports.TimingTransport - Simplifies the implemtation of timing API calls
     * SoftLayer.fixture_client.FixtureClient -> FixtureTransport - simplifies the implementation of fixturing a client
     * CliClient -> /dev/null
     * SoftLayer.transports.make_xml_rpc_api_call -> SoftLayer.transports.XmlRpcTransport - the default transport
     * SoftLayer.transports.make_rest_api_call -> SoftLayer.transports.RestTransport - the transport used to hit the metadata service (potentially default in the future)
     * SoftLayer.testing.MockableTransport - Adds ability to mock specific API endpoints.
    
    The interface for a transport is a callable which takes SoftLayer.transport.Request as the only argument.
    As part of this change, calls(), assert_called_with() and set_mock() methods were added to the TestCase class
     in order to help mock and test. The previous way of mocking relied on the fact that the callable returned
     with client['SERVICE'].METHOD was also a mock object. This can't be the case with the way transports are
     implemented, so this required updating nearly every test.
    
    calls(service_name, method_name) - returns all calls matching the service and method name (both arguments are optional).
    assert_called_with(service_name, method_name, **attribs) - attribs correspond to SoftLayer.transports.Request object.
    set_mock(service_name, method_name) - returns a mock object which will be called whenever the test client calls that service/method.
    
    This should resolve #435 and #435

commit aa6175c97b98993872261deba9aa322bdbe4476c
Author: Amol Jadhav <amolj.1306@gmail.com>
Date:   2014-03-14 11:54:34 +0530

    Always provided HTTP[S] proxy to `requests`
    
    Earlier, only the protocol of the provided proxy was used to forward it
    to `requests` calls. So, if proxy with `ftp` or non-http[s] provided it
    wouldn't get used while making API calls. This caused us to use provided proxy as HTTP[S] proxy
    regardless of the protocol in the proxy URL itself.

commit 8085217ead3613d20daf0f65f17802e63afa13fe
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-08-20 15:09:02 -0500

    API: Settings are now loaded from a config files
    
    Now when SoftLayer.Client() is called it will check for settings in this order:
     * User-Supplied Arguments
     * Environmental Variables
     * User-supplied config file, ~/softlayer, /etc/softlayer.conf
    
    Once the configuration reaches a username and api_key it will stop gathering settings
    and use the settings it has thus far.
    
    CLI: Lots of config logic was taken out of the CLI so it could leverage the
         API configuration that happens automatically.

1	22	SoftLayer/CLI/environment.py

0	37	SoftLayer/tests/CLI/environment_tests.py

commit d21860c1bccd03b4560a50cca532a856003ed33a
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-08-02 15:52:29 -0500

    Adds template support for CCI Creation
    
    This adds the ability to specify a template file to pull in options. The options will
      be merged with CLI-entered options with preference given to the CLI. An example of
      a CCI template is in SoftLayer/tests/fixtures/sample_template.conf.
    
    Example template:
    hostname = myhost
    domain = example.com
    datacenter = dal05
    cpu = 4
    memory = 1024
    os = DEBIAN_7_64
    network = 100
    hourly = true
    monthly= false
    
    Example usage:
      sl cci create --template=test_template.cfg
      sl cci create --os=DEBIAN_7_64 --cpu=2 --template=test_template.cfg

commit fa3ff40a7301143dda6102529d4ce6e62ad46ac9
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-07-22 11:36:31 -0500

    Adds Password Auth to CLI Configuration
    
    This change introduces the ability for 'sl config setup' to be given your
    username/password and it will go out and grab your API key or generate one if
    one does not exist.
    
     * Moves format_output to SoftLayer.CLI.helpers
     * API Key/Password input is masked
    
    Example Usage:
    
    $ sl config setup
    Username: someuser
    API Key or Password:
    Endpoint URL [https://api.softlayer.com/xmlrpc/v3/]:
    :..............:..................................................................:
    :         Name : Value                                                            :
    :..............:..................................................................:
    :     Username : someuser                                                         :
    :      API Key : oyVmeipYQCNrjVS4rF9bHWV7D75S6pa1fghFl384v7mwRCbHTfuJ8qRORIqoVnha :
    : Endpoint URL : https://api.softlayer.com/xmlrpc/v3/                             :
    :..............:..................................................................:
    Are you sure you want to write settings to "/Users/username/.softlayer"? [Y/n]: y

commit 879177afd7ffcb1756b31706bfdb714ce8ee4566
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-06-14 20:31:37 -0500

    Adds Token-based Auth
    
    This adds the ability to use username/password based auth to get an
    auth token to use for subsequent calls.
    
      import SoftLayer
      client = SoftLayer.Client()
      client.authenticate_with_password('username', 'password')
    
      import SoftLayer
      client = SoftLayer.Client()
      # Get all security questions (you basically pick one at random that you have answered)
      client['User_Security_Question'].getAllObjects()
      client.authenticate_with_password('username', 'password', 122, '2004')
    
    note: this is pending an API release to add this feature to the XML-RPC API.

commit b5948459a2467b8c69db393bc4084149ba22f851
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-05-17 14:02:41 -0500

    Refactor of CLI core.
    
    Refactors core CLI code in order to make help a first-class module and
    give more verbose error messages when the module or command is not found.
    
    Example:
    > sl help
    <help about all modules>
    > sl help cci
    <help about all cci commands>
    > sl help cci list
    <help about the cci list command>
    > sl invalid
    <primary help block>
    
    Invalid module: "invalid".
    > sl cci invalid
    <cci module help block>
    
    Invalid command: "invalid".

commit 720004b319513cb291844d7db15def59c0da06bd
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-03-21 16:36:41 -0500

    CCI Commands which require an id now take 'identifier'
    
    CLI: Now instead of requiring the user to remember or copy/paste numeric ids
         everywhere in the CCI-related CLI commands, you can now pass in hostname,
         public ip, private ip or, of course, the numeric id of the CCI.
    
         If no CCIs match, an error is returned.
         If more than one CCI matches, an error is returned with the list of relavent ids.
    
    Examples:
        sl cci detail production
        sl cci dns sync devapp01
        sl cci reboot 12.34.56
        sl cci shutdown 12345

commit d3dbc2286f1867bf1013151e5d1b7e127acdff5d
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-03-19 15:09:11 -0500

    Adds more documentation about filters
    
    * Adds 'filters' module so that 'sl help filters' will output help text
      about how to use filters
    * adds reference to 'sl help filters' in 'sl cci list' help text.
    * makes filters easier to use. The space is not required in between the
      operation and the query value. For example '>2' will work as a filter.

commit 032b6cd502afa5fd5edc652d34ba145e2a231059
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-03-19 10:18:28 -0500

    Removes left padding for raw format
    
    For raw format, tables had a leading space. This causes some weirdness with awk columns.
    Old:
     12345  dal05  something.host.com   4  4096  87.65.43.22  12.34.56.78
     54321  sjc01  something2.host.com  1  1024  12.34.56.88  87.65.43.21
    
    New:
    $ sl cci list --format=raw
    12345  dal05  something.host.com   4  4096  87.65.43.22  12.34.56.78
    54321  sjc01  something2.host.com  1  1024  12.34.56.88  87.65.43.21

commit 1effdde637a46b6d39c7894728a831b981b83367
Author: Tim Ariyeh <tim.ariyeh@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-03-13 18:13:41 -0500

    Clarify CCI transaction output
    
    * Rename the "provisioning" column to "active_transaction"
    It's slightly more accurate, and it's just a preference of mine not to
    introduce new terminology. If users interact with the API in other ways,
    it'll be called a transaction, right? Or is the terminology changing
    globally?
    
    * Display "<None>" for an empty active transaction
    The empty string means that transaction would always have to be the last
    column, because you couldn't count on awk column offsets in selecting
    individual fields. Also, it makes it hard to grep for CCI that _don't_
    currently have an active transaction.

Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-03-13 10:46:09 -0500

    Adds Result Generator for API calls.
    
    This allows for iterating over a set of results in chunks so you don't have to
    transfer and then hold the entire dataset in memory.
    
    >>> cci_iter = client['Account'].getVirtualGuests(iter=True, chunk=100, ...)
    >>> for cci in cci_iter:
    >>>     print cci['fqdn']
    
    Still needs tests.

    Add cci dns sync
    
    CLI: adds 'sl cci dns sync'
    
    usage: sl cci dns sync [-h] [--a] [--ptr] [--really] instance
    
    Sync hostname to A and PTR records
    
    positional arguments:
      instance      Instance ID
    
    optional arguments:
      -h, --help    show this help message and exit
      --a, --A      Sync only the A record
      --ptr, --PTR  Sync only the PTR record
      --really, -y  Confirm all prompt actions

    Adds human readable format for memory.
    
    * CLI: The display of memory in `cci details` and `cci list` with the 'table'
           format (default) will display humanized RAM sizes '1G', '2G', '3G'.

           that can return a PrettyTable from a Table instance. This decouples the
           library code from our use of it. The new way support alignment, sorting,
           formatting columns and formatting specific row entries.

commit 0184b62d05c455bcc1c87deb2d8032a43169774d
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-01-30 14:24:11 -0600

    Creates more granular exceptions v2
    
    The Exception hierarchy is as follows:
    * SoftLayerError
      * SoftLayerAPIError
        * ParseError
          * NotWellFormed
          * UnsupportedEncoding
          * InvalidCharacter
        * ServerError
          * SpecViolation
          * MethodNotFound
          * InvalidMethodParameters
          * InternalError
        * ApplicationError
        * RemoteSystemError
        * TransportError
    
    Reference for standard xmlrpc fault codes: http://xmlrpc-epi.sourceforge.net/specs/rfc.fault_codes.php

28	0	SoftLayer/exceptions.py
10	9	SoftLayer/transport/requests_transport.py
10	9	SoftLayer/transport/xmlrpclib_transport.py

commit 34878dbe3f8400aa18ac9dda63dc3fdd61dae9db
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-01-30 13:53:44 -0600

    Creates more granular exceptions
    
    This allows more fine control over which exceptions you can catch
    with (hopefully) less string introspection. These exceptions have both
    faultCode and faultString from the XML-RPC faults..
    
    The Exception hierarchy is as follows:
    * SoftLayerError
    ** SoftLayerAPIError
    *** ParseError
    *** ServerError
    *** ApplicationError
    *** RemoteSystemError
    *** TransportError
    
    These exceptions are thrown in accordance to XML-RPC spec.
     http://xmlrpc-epi.sourceforge.net/specs/rfc.fault_codes.php

commit a140c2f9d673ff5e41a4ace970bcaadca2ccc714
Author: Kevin McDonald <k3vinmcdonald@gmail.com>
Date:   2013-01-18 11:02:51 -0600

    Adjustment so Tox works with Python3
    
    The 2to3 tool runs against the code and dumps the updated code into the
    build directory. Because of this, 'tests' was added to packages in the setup.py
    file. This change moves tests under SoftLayer and removes it from the setup.py.
    This change also removes Python 2.4 and 2.5 from the tox file.

commit 4ad879ebb24237e2110ff1e19dcf164ac00e0c46
Author: SoftLayer <sldn@softlayer.com>
Date:   2010-07-05 22:23:11 -0500

    Support for SoftLayer's public network endpoints.
    
    The SoftLayer.API.Client class now defaults to use the public network
    endpoints. Pass an optional fourth parameter to the constructor
    specifying the API endpoint you wish to use. The API_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT and
    API_PRIVATE_ENDPOINT constants define the public and private network
    endpoints for the SoftLayer API.
